    create table allocation_requests (
        current_total_allocation integer not null,
        proposed_end_date date,
        proposed_start_date date not null,
        requested_allocation integer not null,
        approver_id bigint not null,
        created_at timestamp(6),
        employee_id bigint not null,
        id bigint generated by default as identity,
        project_id bigint not null,
        requester_id bigint not null,
        resolved_at timestamp(6),
        team_id bigint not null,
        updated_at timestamp(6),
        approver_comments TEXT,
        rejection_reason TEXT,
        request_reason TEXT,
        role_in_team varchar(255) not null,
        status varchar(255) not null check (status in ('PENDING','APPROVED','REJECTED','WITHDRAWN','AUTO_APPROVED')),
        primary key (id)
    )
Hibernate: 
    create table designations (
        level integer not null unique,
        id bigint generated by default as identity,
        dashboard_type varchar(255) not null check (dashboard_type in ('INDIVIDUAL','MANAGER','LEADERSHIP')),
        display_name varchar(255) not null,
        name varchar(255) not null unique,
        primary key (id)
    )
Hibernate: 
    create table employees (
        date_of_joining date,
        is_active boolean not null,
        created_at timestamp(6),
        designation_id bigint not null,
        id bigint generated by default as identity,
        performance_manager_id bigint,
        reporting_manager_id bigint,
        updated_at timestamp(6),
        department varchar(255) not null,
        email varchar(255) not null unique,
        emp_code varchar(255) not null unique,
        first_name varchar(255) not null,
        last_name varchar(255) not null,
        location varchar(255),
        phone varchar(255),
        profile_pic_url varchar(255),
        primary key (id)
    )
Hibernate: 
    create table feedbacks (
        is_anonymous boolean not null,
        rating integer,
        created_at timestamp(6),
        from_employee_id bigint not null,
        id bigint generated by default as identity,
        project_id bigint,
        to_employee_id bigint not null,
        content TEXT not null,
        type varchar(255) not null check (type in ('PEER','UPWARD','DOWNWARD','SELF')),
        primary key (id)
    )
Hibernate: 
    create table notifications (
        is_read boolean,
        created_at timestamp(6),
        id bigint generated by default as identity,
        recipient_id bigint not null,
        reference_id bigint,
        message varchar(1000),
        reference_type varchar(255),
        title varchar(255),
        type varchar(255),
        primary key (id)
    )
Hibernate: 
    create table performance_reviews (
        rating integer not null,
        review_date date,
        created_at timestamp(6),
        employee_id bigint not null,
        id bigint generated by default as identity,
        reviewer_id bigint not null,
        updated_at timestamp(6),
        comments TEXT,
        goals TEXT,
        review_cycle varchar(255) not null,
        status varchar(255) not null check (status in ('DRAFT','SUBMITTED','ACKNOWLEDGED','COMPLETED')),
        primary key (id)
    )
Hibernate: 
    create table projects (
        end_date date,
        start_date date not null,
        created_at timestamp(6),
        engagement_manager_id bigint,

        client_name varchar(255),
        description TEXT,
        name varchar(255) not null,
        project_code varchar(255) not null unique,
        status varchar(255) not null check (status in ('ACTIVE','COMPLETED','ON_HOLD','PIPELINE')),

        primary key (id)
    )

        or tm1_0.employee_id=?

        ? rows
